		if (@sha1_file('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml') !== '9a08836cb73d6cb2897df2e6708da2b191cf1816') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_65();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml') !== '1b811ace0199ce4bfddc6ef322f21e5871f4449d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/sqlSlang/sqlite/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 391\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 391') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
